Topic: Logic
Context: There are 6 scholars F, G, J, L, M, and N, who will speak at a logical meeting, and the speeches are arranged in the following order? (1) Each speaker speaks only once, and only once at the same time By.(2) Three speakers speak before lunch, and the other three speak after lunch.(3) G must speak before lunch.(4) Only one speaker is between M and N.(5) F speaks in the first or third place.
Question: If the speeches of M and N are separated by lunch, which of the following lists all speakers that can be arranged between M and N?
Choices:
  A: G, J
  C: F, G, J
  B: J, L
  D: F, G, J, L
Response 0:
Thought:
  M and N are separated by lunch, which means they are not speaking consecutively.
  From (4), we know that only one speaker is between M and N.
  Therefore, either M or N is the first speaker before lunch, and the other is the first speaker after lunch.
  From (2), we know that three speakers speak before lunch, and the other three speak after lunch.
  Therefore, the other two speakers before lunch are G and J, and the other two speakers after lunch are F and L.
  From (5), we know that F speaks in the first or third place, which means F cannot be the speaker between M and N.
  Therefore, the only possible arrangement is M, G, N or N, G, M.
  The speakers that can be arranged between M and N are J and L.
  The answer is B: J, L.
Action: Answer("B")

  F speaks in the first or third place, so F cannot be between M and N.
  Therefore, the only possible arrangement for the speakers between M and N is J and L.
  The answer is B: J, L.

  A: No one is smart but no wisdom, and no one is smart but not smart.
  B: Most people are smart and wise.
  C: No one is smart and wise.
  D: Most people are neither smart nor wise.

  Option A states that no one is smart but has no wisdom, and no one is smart but not smart. This is possible according to the essayist's statement.
  Option B states that most people are smart and wise. This contradicts the essayist's statement that he has not met anyone who is both smart and wise.
  Option C states that no one is smart and wise. This is possible according to the essayist's statement.
  Option D states that most people are neither smart nor wise. This is not mentioned in the essayist's statement.
  Therefore, the option that cannot be true is B: Most people are smart and wise.

  A: unconfirmed
  B: 9 people
  C: 6 people
  D: 3 people

  A: If changes in prices result in changes in total income and prices in the same direction, then demand is elastic.

(1) G must be performed in the third week.(2) O and S cannot perform continuously.(3) K must be arranged before J and S.(4) F and J must be arranged to perform in two consecutive weeks.

  A: the second week
  B: Fourth week
  C: fifth week
  D: Seventh week
